<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поджарый.html>поджа́рый</a> (18700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджарый.html>поджа́рый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžáryj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>lean, wiry, sinewy</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жа́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>рый</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-поджар-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a> (6325)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tuck up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сидеть.html>сиде́ть</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́в</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sidétʹ, <b>podžáv</b> nogi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sit with one's legs tucked up beneath one</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвост.html>хвост</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podžátʹ</b> xvost</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have one's tail between one's legs</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podžátʹ guby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to purse one's lips, press up one's lips</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tuck in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>подожми́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:живот.html>живо́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podožmi živót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tuck in your stomach</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:берег.html>берегу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódku <b>podžálo</b> k beregu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat was pressed/pushed close to the bank</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tighten</li>
<li>to put/exert pressure <i>(on)</i>, to press, to put the screws <i>(on)</i></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to reap, to harvest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поджина́ть</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поджигатель.html>поджига́тель</a> (27444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджигать.html>поджига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podžigátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set on fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">er</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджигатель.html>поджига́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžigátelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджигатель.html>поджига́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджигатель.html>поджига́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджигатель.html>поджига́телей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поджига́тельница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>arsonist <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">one who has committed the act of arson, or illegally setting fire to property</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жига́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджигать.html>поджига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджечь.html>подже́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to set on fire, to set fire (to), to ignite</li></ol>

***поджидать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поджидать.html>поджида́ть</a> (7054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджидать.html>поджида́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžidátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wait</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie in wait</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:подождать.html>подожда́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>под-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-жид-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***поджимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ть</a> (15316)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podžimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tuck up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>губы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podžimátʹ guby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to purse one's lips, press up one's lips</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tuck in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tighten
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podžimátʹ</b> gájku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten a nut on the bolt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put/exert pressure <i>(on)</i>, to press, to put the screws <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поставщик.html>поставщики́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ют</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">postavščikí nas <b>podžimájut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the suppliers are putting pressure on us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срок.html>сро́ки</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ют</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sróki <b>podžimájut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">time presses</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поджимать.html>поджима́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:поджать.html>поджа́ть</a>.

***подиум.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подиум.html>по́диум</a> (23144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">podium</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подиум.html>по́диум</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pódium</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подиум.html>по́диума</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подиум.html>по́диумы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подиум.html>по́диумов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>raised floor, podium, platform, stage, runway</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a> (9379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">под-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pod-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:катить.html>кати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">katítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkatítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатывать.html>подка́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(to)</i>, to drive <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to roll up <i>(to)</i>, to drive up <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самому</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подъезд.html>подъе́зду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>podkatítʹ</b> k samomu podʺjézdu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drive right up to the front door</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(emotions)</i> to rise <i>(in)</i>, to fill, to seize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдцу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тревога.html>трево́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k sérdcu u menjá <b>podkatíla</b> trevóga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I was suddenly filled with apprehension/anxiety</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ком</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рлу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó kom <b>podkatíl</b> k górlu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he felt a lump rise in his throat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***подкатывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:подкатывать.html>подка́тывать</a> (17825)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">podkatítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатывать.html>подка́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">podkátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подкатить.html>подкати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll <i>(to)</i>, to drive <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to roll up <i>(to)</i>, to drive up <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><i>(emotions)</i> to rise <i>(in)</i>, to fill, to seize</li></ol>
